# Architecture Directory

Architecture-level documentation for niov-foundation. This
directory holds Architecture Decision Records (ADRs) — the
captured rationale behind every load-bearing architectural
choice in the codebase. ADRs explain *why* a decision was made,
not *what* was made (the codebase is the source of truth for
the *what*; ADRs prevent re-litigation of the *why*).

This directory is distinct from:

- `docs/reference/` — substrate documentation (glossary,
  architectural-anchors catalog, section-progress trackers)
- `docs/contributing/` — contributor guides (code style,
  testing, multi-LLM operation)

## Directory Structure

```
docs/architecture/
├── README.md                           (this file — index)
└── decisions/
    ├── 0000-template.md                (ADR template + how-to)
    ├── 0001-three-wallet-architecture.md
    ├── 0002-append-only-audit-chain.md
    ├── 0003-frozen-config-tamper-anchors.md
    ├── 0004-service-owned-auth-gate.md
    ├── 0005-no-console-in-apps-api-src.md
    ├── 0006-cross-org-leak-prevention.md
    ├── 0007-manual-bearer-auth-compliance-endpoints.md
    ├── 0008-entity-compliance-profile-org-level.md
    ├── 0009-cosmp-seven-operation-enumeration.md
    └── 0010-foundation-tests-legitimately-slow.md
```

## Architectural Decision Records (ADRs)

ADRs use the Michael Nygard format with niov-foundation
extensions (Easier/Harder consequence split, bidirectional
citation block, ISO-dated Status). The template at
`decisions/0000-template.md` includes both the structure and
the "How To Use This Template" guidance for new ADRs.

ADR catalog as of [BEAM-COSMP-INTEROP-ADR] (2026-05-13;
37 ADRs):

- **ADR-0001** — Three-wallet architecture (foundational)
- **ADR-0002** — Append-only audit chain with BEFORE DELETE trigger (foundational)
- **ADR-0003** — Frozen-config tamper anchors (Section 12C.0)
- **ADR-0004** — Service-owned auth gate pattern (Section 12C.0)
- **ADR-0005** — No `console.*` in `apps/api/src` (Section 12C.0; DRIFT 2 Option C)

- **ADR-0007** — Manual bearer auth for `/compliance/*` endpoints (Section 12C.0; will be superseded by Sub-box 7)

- **ADR-0009** — COSMP 7-operation enumeration (locked by patent US 12,517,919)

- **ADR-0050** — GOVSEC.5 Break-Glass / Time-Boxed Audit (GOVSEC.5 design-first ADR for GAP-K1 — break-glass is greenfield; **no code in the ADR phase**; locks the design before any implementation. Model: a time-boxed emergency grant — not a permanent role, not a general bypass, **not a self-approval**; invoked with explicit justification; scoped to a specific privileged action/route; **mandatory `valid_until`** (no perpetual access). Scope: the 4 dual-control `PRIVILEGED_ENDPOINTS` routes initially (broader org-admin set is a separate follow-on). Dual-control relationship: normal path remains dual-control; break-glass is a constrained emergency alternative; the GAP-C1 self-approval guard (`caller === source_entity_id` forbidden) remains intact; chosen relationship = authorized invoke + short time-box + **mandatory post-hoc two-person audit/review** (or second-actor-before-activation, EXECUTE-QLOCK-selected). Audit: future append-only literals (`BREAK_GLASS_INVOKED`/`USED`/`EXPIRED`/`REVIEWED`) in `audit.ts` — **no ADR-0002 amendment** for additive literals (G4-B1/Sub-box-3/ADR-0042 precedent). Schema: a future `BreakGlassGrant`-style table mirroring `LawfulBasis` (mandatory `valid_until`); `EscalationRequest.expires_at` is insufficient (it time-boxes approval validity, not an emergency access grant). RULE 21 research arc embedded (NIST SP 800-53 AC-3/AC-6/AU-6/AU-12 + NIST SP 800-207 ZTA + JIT access + break-glass PAM/HIPAA best practice + SOC 2 CC6 / ISO 27001 A.5.18 + LawfulBasis precedent). GAP-K1 = designed/not-closed; **GOVSEC.5 remains OPEN** (code + audit-completeness tests required to close); GAP-O7 open; D2-C/GOVSEC.7 deferred. cites RULE 0 + RULE 11 + RULE 12 + RULE 13 + RULE 20 + RULE 21 + ADR-0049 + ADR-0026 + ADR-0036 + ADR-0002; **Status: Accepted 2026-05-22** (Proposed 2026-05-22 at `[GOVSEC-GOVERNMENT-GRADE-HARDENING-GOVSEC5-BREAK-GLASS-TIMEBOXED-AUDIT-ADR-AUTH]` → Accepted 2026-05-22 at the BG.3 closure cascade `[GOVSEC-GOVERNMENT-GRADE-HARDENING-GOVSEC5-BREAK-GLASS-BG3-CLOSURE-EXECUTE-VERIFY-AUTH]`; **GAP-K1 CLOSED** across ADR-0050 design + BG.1 substrate `2f487fc` + BG.2 live integration `f5f0256` (green CI run `26297686163`); accepted for break-glass / time-boxed audit only — **GOVSEC.5 remains OPEN** pending the org-admin route-set throttle follow-on + GAP-K2 least-privilege review))
- **ADR-0051** — Otzar Chat Transparency and COE-Governed Retrieval Surfacing (Wave 1 Otzar enterprise-experience contract ADR; surfaces the governed context metadata `COE.assembleContext` already produces — items loaded, items skipped for low relevance, items skipped for budget, an `access_limited` boolean, and per-item provenance derived only from already-permitted context items — via an **additive** extension of `conductSession` / `ConductSessionSuccess` at `apps/api/src/services/otzar/otzar.service.ts`; `context_used` + `tokens_consumed` + `response` + `conversation_id` unchanged (backward-compatible); two new OPTIONAL fields `transparency` + `context_provenance`; **no parallel `similarity.service` retrieval path and no COE bypass** — similarity wiring stays deferred to a future Founder-authorized ADR-0022 amendment per ADR-0043 §Q-G3.6-ε; - **ADR-0052** — Otzar Domain General Intelligence and Governed Synchronicity (doctrine ADR; canonicalizes Otzar's product/architecture truth so future build sessions do not drift — adds NO runtime behavior, NO endpoints, NO schema, NO code; long-form companion `docs/otzar/DOMAIN_GENERAL_INTELLIGENCE_DOCTRINE.md`. Locks: (1) Otzar is the governed enterprise intelligence layer on top of Foundation — the operating layer for the Autonomous Enterprise — a bounded **Domain General Intelligence** system inside governed enterprise domains, NOT a generic chatbot/admin-console/workflow-automation/AI-harness/thin-frontend; canonical *"Otzar turns the enterprise itself into a governed collaborative intelligence layer"*; (2) the enterprise/domain is an active knowledge collaborator (enterprise knowledge → scoped AI Twin → human work → team coordination → permissioned updates → enterprise memory improves), not passive storage; (3) RULE 0 sovereignty — no AI accesses human/entity/enterprise data without explicit revocable governed permission, raw unpermitted data never exposed; (4) human↔AI Twin **scope parity** (same RBAC/ABAC boundary, project visibility, tenant boundaries, escalation limits, allowed actions; the Twin is a scoped extension, never above the human, never a spy/manager/uncontrolled actor); (5) *"Otzar does not watch employees to judge them"* — permissioned work observation, NOT surveillance/monitoring/policing; (6) **drift** prevention is first-class; (7) governed best-practice learning (permissioned/scoped/auditable/revocable; no raw-data leakage, no hidden evaluation); (8) scoped Twin-to-Twin coordination through policy-governed channels exchanging only minimum relevant info; (9) *"Otzar can proactively prepare, coordinate, and recommend inside scope; it executes sensitive actions only under permission, policy, or approval"* — no boundary-crossing, no cross-tenant leakage, no hidden autonomy; (10) **Control Tower** is the governance/executive-clarity layer (AI-generated what-happened/why/what-changed/needs-approval/risk/recommended-action summaries), not a classic admin dashboard; (11) reports are *"generated from permissioned operational signals and routed according to hierarchy, scope, and relevance"* — not raw access; executives get summaries without raw unpermitted employee data; (12) multi-tenant + dynamic governed grouping at enterprise scale, each with scoped intelligence; (13) DGI is **bounded** (no global AGI; powerful because governed/scoped inside a domain); (14) **The Governed Synchronicity Loop** (alias Scoped Execution Intelligence Loop): Observe → Understand → Align → Assist → Coordinate → Approve → Execute → Report → Learn → Improve; (15) canonical 15-step build order + sequencing guards (governance before autonomy; web coherence before desktop; context policy before MCP/connectors; transcript ownership/retention/scope policy before raw transcripts; single Twin + scope + approvals before hives; real backend events before dashboards; never fake autonomy); (16) Wave 1 (ADR-0051) is *"the first governed transparency surface in the larger Domain General Intelligence path"*. cites RULE 0 + RULE 1 + RULE 4 + RULE 9 + RULE 13 + RULE 20 + ADR-0051 + ADR-0048 + ADR-0002; companion doctrine `docs/otzar/DOMAIN_GENERAL_INTELLIGENCE_DOCTRINE.md`; Status: **Accepted 2026-05-27** at `[OTZAR-DGI-DOCTRINE-FOUNDATION-DOCS-EXECUTE-VERIFY-AUTH]`)
- **ADR-0053** — Otzar Employee AI Twin Role-Scope Profile and Drift-Prevention Foundations (Wave 2 contract ADR; **design-only — NO code, NO schema, NO endpoints, NO tests**; governed by ADR-0052 build order step 3. Locks: (1) **Wave 2A primary** — additively extend `GET /api/v1/otzar/my-twin` (`apps/api/src/services/otzar/otzar.service.ts` `getMyTwin`) into a richer governed employee AI Twin **role-scope profile**, **self-scoped only** (caller reads only their own twin; no other employees' scope, no cross-tenant data, no raw permission internals/bridge IDs/capability flags/raw clearance, no hidden evaluation, no surveillance framing); (2) **safe derived fields** — identity + role (`role_title`/`job_title`/`department`/`hierarchy_level` if safe) + scope summary (tenant/department labels, membership count, high-level **permission posture label** not raw RBAC/ABAC, approval/escalation posture label) + assistance profile (`autonomy_mode`/`swarm_enabled`/`role_template` status/`skills` if real) + governance (approver relationship; threshold actions require permission/policy/approval; observation is permissioned work context not surveillance) + continuity (recent conversation/correction/learning counts; **no raw transcript content**); new models need a later ADR); (4) **Wave 2B conversation look-back** bounded to metadata+summary only (**no raw transcripts**), locking **`summary_capsule_id` on `OtzarConversation`** as the preferred future additive link (not implemented here); (5) **drift-prevention FOUNDATIONS only** — `CORRECTION` is the first human-alignment primitive (already prioritized in `conductSession` Layer 1); Wave 2A may expose only correction/learning counts + an "alignment signals available" label (no scoring/policing/hidden evaluation); full **drift** detection (recurring `CORRECTION` → `IntelligencePattern` write-side, stale-context warnings, drift-signal contract, proactive suggestions) is Wave 3; (6) **Control Tower** consumption deferred (no fake dashboards); (7) sequencing — **Foundation role/scope profile contract first**, then Foundation tests, then Control Tower My Twin UI second, look-back third, drift after; (8) non-goals — no autonomy/execution-engine/MCP/raw-transcripts/listener-sidecar/hives/Agent-Playground/desktop/Twin-to-Twin/Control-Tower-reports/notifications/**employee surveillance**/productivity-policing/hidden-evaluation/cross-tenant-leakage/raw-unpermitted-data/fake-capability-claims; acceptance criteria = additive/backward-compatible + safe self-scoped + tests proving no internals leak. cites RULE 0 + RULE 1 + RULE 4 + RULE 9 + RULE 13 + RULE 20 + RULE 21 + ADR-0052 + ADR-0051 + ADR-0048 + ADR-0002; - **ADR-0054** — Otzar Conversation Look-back and Safe Continuity Surfacing (Wave 2B contract ADR; **design-only — no code/endpoints; no schema migration in this phase**; governed by ADR-0052 build-order step 4. Locks: (1) NEW self-scoped detail endpoint **`GET /api/v1/otzar/conversations/:id`** (bearer + `read`; caller reads only conversations where `OtzarConversation.entity_id` == authenticated entity); (2) **minimal additive response** — `conversation_id`/`twin_id`/`source_type`/`status`/`started_at`/`closed_at`/`message_count`/`summary`/`topics`/`summary_available`/`summary_capsule_id`/`detail_availability`/`transparency_available`/`continuity_note`; (3) `detail_availability` enum **`SUMMARY_AVAILABLE` | `NO_SUMMARY_YET` | `ACTIVE_NOT_CLOSED`**; (4) `summary` derived ONLY from the linked `CONVERSATION_LEARNING` capsule `payload_summary`, `topics` only from its `topic_tags`; pre-existing conversations may have `summary_capsule_id = null` — **no backfill**; (5) **additive schema** — add nullable **`summary_capsule_id String? @db.Uuid`** to `OtzarConversation` (implements the ADR-0053 §4 preferred explicit link; retires fragile `storage_location` string-parse / D-OTZ-3); (6) `closeConversation` sets `summary_capsule_id` to the created CONVERSATION_LEARNING capsule id; (7) safe boundary — **no raw transcripts / messages / prompts / chain-of-thought / raw context / vectors / permission internals / bridge IDs / capability flags / cross-tenant data / fake retrospective transparency / fake corrections / fake continuity**; `summary` is a close summary, NOT a transcript; (8) honest deferred — `transparency_available` is **always false** (ADR-0051 transparency is live **response-only**, not persisted); `continuity_note` states per-conversation correction/transparency signals are not retained; `corrections_count`/`context_provenance`/`access_limited` excluded (not linked/not persisted); **do not fabricate** for past conversations; (9) access — cross-caller → `NOT_CONVERSATION_OWNER`, unknown id → `CONVERSATION_NOT_FOUND`, reuse existing `OtzarFailure` codes, no new audit literal; (10) migration via `db:push:test` per ADR-0025 (never bare `prisma db push`); (11) test reqs incl. wire-level no-leak + self-scope; (12) order — ADR → schema → closeConversation link → mapper → `getConversationDetail` service → route → tests → merge Foundation first → Control Tower later; (13)/(14) Control Tower detail UI later (metadata + summary + topics + honest "not retained" note; no raw transcripts); non-goals — raw transcript persistence/UI, listeners, MCP/connectors, hives, Agent Playground, autonomous execution, enterprise reporting, full audit viewer, dashboards-without-events, billing, per-conversation transparency persistence, conversation→correction linkage. cites RULE 0 + RULE 1 + RULE 4 + RULE 9 + RULE 13 + RULE 20 + RULE 21 + ADR-0053 + ADR-0051 + ADR-0052 + ADR-0002 (operational refs ADR-0042 + ADR-0025); - **ADR-0055** — Otzar Correction Signals and Drift-Prevention Continuity (Wave 2C contract ADR; **design-only — no code/endpoints; no schema migration in this phase**; governed by ADR-0052 build-order steps 5–6 + closes ADR-0054's explicitly-deferred `conversation→correction linkage` non-goal. Locks: (1) **Scope** — Wave 2C links correction submissions to conversation continuity and exposes per-conversation correction-signal counts + freshness through a safe self-scoped sub-resource; does NOT implement full drift detection / drift score / stale-context warnings / proactive suggestions / `IntelligencePattern` auto-write / org-wide aggregation / manager dashboards / employee scoring / autonomous execution / transcript replay / listeners / MCP / hives / Agent Playground / enterprise reporting / billing / full audit viewer; (2) **additive schema** — add nullable **`conversation_id String? @db.Uuid`** to `MemoryCapsule` + `@@index([wallet_id, capsule_type, conversation_id])`; no backfill; no new model; no new enum; no new audit literal; no FK constraint (service code owns existence + self-scope checks per Section 9); pre-existing `CORRECTION` capsules remain `conversation_id = null`; (3) **extend `POST /api/v1/otzar/correction`** — body adds OPTIONAL `conversation_id`; omitted → backward-compatible (persists null); provided → service validates ownership; unknown → `CONVERSATION_NOT_FOUND` (404); cross-caller → `NOT_CONVERSATION_OWNER` (403); on success the resulting `CORRECTION` capsule stores `conversation_id`; (4) **NEW** `GET /api/v1/otzar/conversations/:id/corrections` — bearer + `read`; self-scoped; cross-caller / unknown id same codes; reuse existing `OtzarFailure` codes; no new audit literal; (5) **safe response** — `{ ok, conversation_id, corrections_count, has_corrections, last_correction_at, drift_prevention_note, continuity_note }`; `corrections_count` is a real Prisma count of `capsule_type='CORRECTION'` + caller's wallet + `conversation_id = :id` + `deleted_at IS NULL`; `last_correction_at` is ISO `created_at` of the most-recent linked capsule or null; (6) **forbidden response fields** — raw correction `payload_summary`/`payload_content`; correction capsule IDs list; `target_capsule_id`; target capsule content; transcripts; raw messages/prompts/chain-of-thought/raw context; `storage_location`; `content_hash`; vectors; embeddings; permission-envelope internals; bridge IDs; capability flags; other users' / cross-tenant data; drift score; employee score; best-practice learned/applied status; manager visibility fields; org-wide aggregation; (7) **submitted vs learned/applied** — Wave 2C surfaces ONLY submitted/available correction signals (counts + last-seen); MUST NOT claim "best practice learned" / "behavior permanently fixed" / "drift prevented" / "AI fixed itself"; Layer 1 priority + `RELEVANCE_MAX` propagation are real but described as scoped correction priority within the caller's wallet, not autonomous learning; (8) **`ConversationDetailView` UNCHANGED** — ADR-0054 surface is not modified; `transparency_available` stays false; corrections live on the new `/corrections` sub-resource; (9) **safe frontend language** locks allowed copy ("Correction signals" / "Corrections linked to this conversation" / "Not enough correction history yet" / "This does not expose raw messages." / "This is not an employee score." / "This is not a transcript.") and forbidden copy ("drift score" / "employee score" / "manager monitoring" / "surveillance" / "full history" / "message replay" / "best practice learned" / "AI fixed itself" / "autonomous drift prevention" / "all corrections across the org"); (10) access self-scoped throughout (no manager/admin/org-wide read path); (11) migration via `db:push:test` per ADR-0025 (never bare `prisma db push`); local DB reconciliation per ADR-0035 §38 / ADR-0047 PR.3 if needed; (12) cross-language boundary — Prisma owns `conversation_id`; Ecto schema NOT extended (ADR-0033 Q-G3-θ / G3.8 precedent); (13) test reqs — `processCorrection` persists `conversation_id` valid / backward-compat null / 404 unknown / 403 cross-caller; `GET …/corrections` real count + zero state + 403 cross-caller + 404 unknown + wire no-leak; ADR-0054 detail regression green; `getMyTwin` `recent_correction_count` regression green; Layer 1 fixture green; RULE 16 + 12-error typecheck baseline preserved; repo-approved vitest tier configs (ADR-0035 §37); (14) implementation order — ADR → schema → `POST /correction` extend → pure mapper → `getConversationCorrections` service → `GET …/corrections` route → tests → merge Foundation first → Control Tower later. cites RULE 0 + RULE 1 + RULE 4 + RULE 9 + RULE 13 + RULE 20 + RULE 21 + ADR-0054 + ADR-0053 + ADR-0052 + ADR-0051 + ADR-0025 + ADR-0002 (operational refs ADR-0033 + ADR-0035 + ADR-0042 + ADR-0047); Patent-implementation evidence — US 12,517,919 (COSMP) + US 12,164,537 (DMW) + US 12,399,904 (scoped wallet-bound continuity; no cross-tenant fusion); Status: **Accepted 2026-05-27** at `[OTZAR-WAVE-2C-ADR-0055-CORRECTION-CONVERSATION-LINKAGE-WRITE-AND-ACCEPT-AUTH]`)

- **ADR-0065** — Agent Playground Long-Term Product Vision — DGI Enterprise Scenario Playground (Section 5 Wave 3 product-vision ADR; **design-only; NEW ADR sitting ABOVE ADR-0060 at the product-vision tier**; does NOT modify ADR-0060 which remains the canonical Wave 2 implementation contract for the first backend substrate / inspector foundation. multi-agent scenario exploration; organizational decision simulation; alternative plan comparison; outcome comparison; best-path recommendation; governed transition from simulation to Action runtime; analogous to DeepMind-style scenario exploration adapted for the governed enterprise with humans in the loop at every material decision. 12 sub-decisions: §1 long-term purpose statement canonical; §2 13-input canonical set the future scenario engine MAY consume (org goals, role-scoped context, approved working sets, ActionPolicy/governance_terms constraints, connector capabilities, Hive/team context, audit-derived operational signals, enterprise analytics aggregates, prior corrections/drift signals, approved memory capsules, dependency/blocker/cost/timing/risk/impact estimations) — every input scope-bounded by existing Foundation primitives; - **ADR-0080** — Out-of-the-Box Role, Tool, Workflow, Connector, and Dandelion Onboarding Ontology for Digital Twins (design-only) (Responds to Section 10 production-readiness audit PR #164 launch-blocker: Otzar is substrate-strong but role-naive out of the box. Foundation governance authorizes."). §2 decision (16 design objects: RoleTemplate / DepartmentTemplate / CompanyTemplate / ToolProfile / WorkflowTemplate / ConnectorPreset / DelegatedAuthorityProfile / PermissionBundle / OnboardingQuestionSet / AhaMomentPack / SafeFallbackMode / OrgChartRelationshipTemplate / IndustryVariant / CompanySizeVariant / DandelionFlowTemplate / DigitalTwinStarterProfile). §3 13-item non-goals catalog. §4 existing-Dandelion distinction (today's `dandelion.service.ts` = org-admin Phase 0/2/3/4 invite/seating; first real Section 4 connector selected from matrix NOT founder intuition; candidate-evaluation surface enumerated but first-connector decision DEFERRED). §11 governance and safety (templates are defaults NOT identity claims; Dandelion suggestions NOT permissions; Foundation governance authorizes per RULE 0 + ADR-0027; no sensitive/protected-attribute inference; no employee scoring; no manager surveillance per ADR-0052 + ADR-0058; no unapproved write actions per ADR-0026; read-only-first for sensitive systems; delegated authority explicit; dual-control where needed; all connector actions audited via existing ADMIN_ACTION + INVOKE_CONNECTOR lineage NO NEW LITERAL; regulator-ready posture preserved per ADR-0070 neutral compliance vocabulary). §12 mapping to 10 sections (Section 1 starter Twin context via ADR-0048; Section 2 WorkflowTemplate → governed Actions per ADR-0057; Section 3 DepartmentTemplate.default_hive_patterns shapes Hives per ADR-0059; Section 4 ToolProfile + ConnectorPreset drive connector prioritization; Section 5 RoleTemplate + WorkflowTemplate seed scenarios per ADR-0060 + ADR-0076; Section 6 KPIs inform aggregates per ADR-0061; Section 7 audit visible per ADR-0071; Section 8 packaging input (Founder decision pending); Section 9 admin manages templates; Section 10 Dandelion reduces deployment friction). §13 implementation ladder (Wave 1 this ADR design-only; Wave 2 static seed catalog with EA worked example deepest; Wave 3 CT/Dandelion preview READ-ONLY; Wave 4 onboarding recommendation engine SUGGEST-ONLY; Wave 5 DigitalTwinStarterProfile attachment; Wave 6 connector-priority matrix output; Wave 7 first real connector with RULE 21 research arc; Wave 8 continuous adaptation per ADR-0048 — each subsequent wave requires its own Founder authorization at slice; ADR-0080 does NOT pre-authorize Waves 2-8). §14 consequences (positive: Otzar no longer starts blank + grounded connector strategy + Dandelion coherent activation layer + faster aha moment + safer defaults + closes one Section 10 hard launch blocker at architecture register + RULE 0 sovereignty preserved + regulator-ready posture preserved; tradeoffs: large ontology surface + seed catalog quality critical + over-templating risk if not overrideable + governance discipline required per wave + industry/company-size variants open-ended + existing dandelion.service.ts divergence risk + ADR is large no shortcut). §15 citations + RULE 14 bidirectional discipline (RULE 0/1/4/9/10/13/14/20/21 + ADR-0001/0024/0026/0027/0033/0034/0036/0046/0048/0050/0052/0057/0058/0059/0060/0061/0069/0070/0071/0076/0078/0079 + Patent US 12,517,919 + US 12,164,537 + US 12,399,904). §16 Founder authorization at `[FOUNDER-ADR-0080-OOTB-DANDELION-ONTOLOGY-DESIGN-ONLY-AUTH]` 2026-06-01; - **ADR-0079** — Transcript Substrate Policy for Conversation Context Signals (design-only Policy ADR) (**Required policy prerequisite for ADR-0078 Stage 1+ implementation per ADR-0078 §6C.13**. Turns ADR-0078 §6 (12 implementation prerequisites) + §6A (19 transcript-governance capabilities) + §6B (4 canonical access tiers — Internal Enterprise / Compliance-Legal / Regulator Evidence Package / External Third-Party — NEVER collapsed) + §6C (capture-eligibility + work-relevance filtering layer that sits architecturally BEFORE Layer 1 ingest) into enforceable policy + service-tier contracts. **No code / schema / new routes / listeners / transcript capture / Control Tower code / LLM / Python / BEAM / connector invocation / Action mutation / new audit literal / raw transcript exposure by default at this commit**. 33 sections: §1 context + ADR-0078 doctrine inheritance verbatim (10 canonical sentences); §2 decision (policy gates for capture/retention/use/search-retrieval/quote-excerpt/redaction/audit/export/regulator-disclosure/deletion-pseudonymization/Agent-Playground-use/permissioned-evidence-drilldown); §3 25-item non-goals catalog; §4 policy scope (Otzar Enterprise transcript substrate only; not consumer/personal-life); §5 capture eligibility (8 pre-Layer-1 gates ALL must pass; failure → Foundation NEVER receives transcript); §6 work-relevance classification (5-class vocab inherited from ADR-0078 §6C.9.a; classifier MUST be biased toward privacy; uncertainty defaults to UNKNOWN_REQUIRES_REVIEW); §7 personal/non-work exclusion (13-category list incl. protected-class + union/labor-organizing where applicable; suppressed at source OR redacted at ingest); §8 mixed-conversation handling (isolate work segment only; redact personal); §9 sensitive-personal handling (BLOCKED from Agent Playground entirely; retain ONLY if legally required + non-indexable); §10 business-purpose binding (UNKNOWN_BUSINESS_PURPOSE blocks Agent Playground; NEVER inferred from mere workplace presence); §11 scope binding (mandatory before retention + signal generation + re-checked at drilldown; ORG_SCOPED is narrowest org-wide scope and STILL requires per-read auth); §12 four canonical access tiers NEVER collapse — §12.1 Internal Enterprise (TAR-authoritative; signals by default + Layer 4 drilldown when authorized; standard audit) + §12.2 Compliance/Legal Review (COMPLIANCE_REVIEW_SCOPED; enhanced audit; privilege-redaction-lift only under attorney-client review; jurisdiction-aware) + §12.3 Regulator-Facing Evidence Package (ADR-0036 LawfulBasis 9-condition gate + export-only NEVER live drilldown + minimum-necessary + dual-control per ADR-0026 RECOMMENDED + NO "regulator approved"/"compliant"/"no fine risk" claims; maximum audit; raw transcript NEVER in audit details) + §12.4 External Third-Party (counterparties/NDAs/discovery; explicit per-party authorization NEVER inferred from same-org TAR; maximum redaction + maximum audit; NEVER signal-generation capability); §13 notice/consent jurisdiction-aware (NOT a substitute for business purpose OR work relevance; consent revocation propagates to derived signals); §14 retention policy (5-class vocab inherited; legal hold overrides deletion; retention NEVER auto-authorizes Agent Playground use; non-indexable mode required; GDPR Article 17 alignment); §15 legal hold (place/release requires authority; dual-control RECOMMENDED per ADR-0026; locks deletion/pseudonymization; NEVER auto-exposes to Agent Playground OR managers); §16 redaction policy (personal/privileged/client-confidential/speaker-pseudonymization/protected-class redaction at ingest; lifting requires tier-appropriate authority + audit; ADR-0078 §3.8 redaction_status 4 values inherited); §17 privileged conversation handling (attorney-client/work-product/in-house-counsel/executive-session NEVER default product surface; compliance/legal tier only); §18 client/customer confidential handling (client/matter scoping; minimum-necessary; NO cross-client/cross-matter leakage); §19 transcript access audit (9 audit event categories: read/search/quote/export/drilldown/redaction-lift/legal-hold/regulator-package/deletion-pseudonymization; ZERO new audit literal — existing ADMIN_ACTION + details.action discriminator pattern reused verbatim; 15 suggested future details.action values listed; raw transcript text NEVER in audit details — only IDs / labels / metadata / hashes); §20 quote/excerpt permission (default surfaces NEVER show exact quotes; Layer 4 drilldown OR approved export only; quote requires purpose + tier + scope re-check + redaction check + audit + minimum-necessary); §21 export/eDiscovery (legal/compliance authority required; scope-limited; bulk export FORBIDDEN; dual-control RECOMMENDED; preserves provenance + correction trail + retention/legal-hold state + redactions + audit); §22 regulator disclosure (ADR-0036 LawfulBasis gate; package-only NEVER live drilldown; ADR-0070 §9 legal-advice boundary inherited; neutral regulated-company framing — regulatory exposure / examination readiness / enforcement risk / supervisory evidence / books-and-records compliance / proactive disclosure / regulator-ready transparency; AVOID charged terms); §23 correction/amendment trail (preserves original provenance via transcript_hash; never silent rewrite; amendment may update signals only through governed reclassification); §24 linkage policy (meeting-to-Action / Decision / Project-timeline / Scenario / Hive / Client-matter; NEVER without business purpose AND scope; personal/sensitive excluded segments NEVER linkage evidence; NEVER manager surveillance OR employee scoring); §25 service-tier contract (9 future service gates ADR-0079 locks at policy register: canCaptureTranscript / classifyConversationRelevance / canRetainTranscript / canUseForAgentPlayground / canDrillDownTranscript / canQuoteTranscript / canExportTranscript / canDiscloseToRegulator / canDeleteOrPseudonymizeTranscript — each with required inputs + allowed outputs + denial reason shape + audit expectations + no-leak expectations); Stage 1 no-leak guard test required across every non-Layer-4 surface); §27 Agent Playground use policy (closed-vocab combinator: allowed when conversation_relevance_class ∈ {WORK_RELEVANT, approved MIXED_WORK_PERSONAL after redaction} + business_purpose_label ≠ UNKNOWN_BUSINESS_PURPOSE + agent_playground_use ∈ {ALLOWED_FOR_SIGNALS, ALLOWED_AFTER_REDACTION, LEGAL_COMPLIANCE_ONLY} + capture_eligibility ∈ {CAPTURE_ALLOWED, CAPTURE_ALLOWED_WITH_REDACTION, CAPTURE_REQUIRED_BY_LEGAL_HOLD} + scope_binding_type set; NEVER NON_WORK_PERSONAL / SENSITIVE_PERSONAL / UNKNOWN_REQUIRES_REVIEW unreviewed / privileged raw / personal-sensitive-under-legal-hold / manager-surveillance / employee-scoring / psychological-profile signals); - **ADR-0078** — Conversation Substrate — Source-of-Truth Transcripts + `conversation_context_signals[]` Safe-Projection Layer for Agent Playground (design-only) (Defines the **four-layer conversation substrate** Otzar Enterprise uses to remember work without surveilling life. **Layer 1** = Raw Transcript Source-of-Truth (governed exact transcripts; speaker attribution where authorized; timestamps; meeting/session metadata; retention/legal-hold; consent/notice; provenance; transcript_text_encrypted at rest per ADR-0019; allowed fields canonical at §4 — `transcript_id`/`source_type`/`meeting_id`/`session_id`/`participant_entity_ids`/`speaker_entity_id`/`start_time`/`end_time`/`transcript_text_encrypted`/`transcript_hash`/`retention_class`/`legal_hold_status`/`access_scope`/`consent_notice_status`/`source_system`/`created_at`/`deleted_at`). **Layer 2** = Scoped Reasoning (Agent Playground Wave 7/Wave 9 may consult Layer 1 internally for accuracy when caller has authority + retrieval is purpose-bound + policy-checked + audited; Layer 2 output flows to Layer 3 projection, NEVER directly to a default response body). **Layer 3** = Safe Projection (`conversation_context_signals[]` closed-vocab/safe-summary/honest-note default UI + reasoning-output substrate). **Layer 4** = Permissioned Evidence Drilldown (authorized users may click signal → transcript excerpt under per-tier authorization re-check; explicit gesture only; purpose-bound; audited; redaction-respecting; scope-narrowing). **Canonical doctrines** (4 sentences): primary "transcripts remain the governed source of truth, while signals provide no-leak decision context"; companion 1 "Exact transcripts are the evidentiary source of truth; `conversation_context_signals[]` are the governed intelligence interface"; companion 2 "Otzar Enterprise should remember work, not surveil life"; companion 3 "The transcript layer preserves authorized business evidence; the relevance layer prevents personal life from becoming enterprise intelligence". **§3 closed vocabularies**: `signal_type` (§3.1; 17 values incl. PRIOR_COMMITMENT_IDENTIFIED / STAKEHOLDER_CONCERN_IDENTIFIED / APPROVAL_DEPENDENCY_IDENTIFIED / CONFLICTING_DIRECTION_IDENTIFIED / MISSING_STAKEHOLDER_INPUT / MEETING_CONTEXT_SUPPORTS_PATH / HUMAN_OBJECTION_REQUIRES_REVIEW / DECISION_OWNER_UNCLEAR / ACTION_ITEM_DEPENDENCY_IDENTIFIED / RISK_RAISED_BY_STAKEHOLDER / DEADLINE_OR_TIMING_CONSTRAINT_IDENTIFIED / CUSTOMER_OR_CLIENT_IMPACT_RAISED / POLICY_OR_COMPLIANCE_CONCERN_RAISED / SECURITY_OR_DATA_SCOPE_CONCERN_RAISED / PRIOR_DECISION_REFERENCED / UNRESOLVED_QUESTION_IDENTIFIED / CONTEXT_INSUFFICIENT_FOR_RECOMMENDATION) + `signal_confidence_label` (§3.2; 4 values) + `signal_source_type` (§3.3; 8 values) + `signal_scope` (§3.4; 6 values) + `TranscriptRef` Layer-4 attachment shape (§3.5; never carries raw content) + `evidence_label` (§3.6; 13 values) + `retention_class` (§3.7; 5 values) + `redaction_status` (§3.8; 4 values) + `policy_purpose` (§3.9; 7 values driving Layer-4 audit + scope). **§6 12 transcript-implementation prerequisites** (participant notice/consent / retention policy / legal hold / role-based access / scope binding / redaction / access audit / export / regulator disclosure / deletion-or-pseudonymization / provenance/timestamp / quote-excerpt permission) — load-bearing for Stage 1+. **§6A 19 transcript-governance capabilities** ADR-0079 MUST cover (notice+consent; speaker attribution; redaction; privileged conversation; client confidential; legal hold; retention schedules; deletion; eDiscovery export; regulator approval; role-based access; project/matter/hive/action scoping; access audit; quote/excerpt audit; correction/amendment trail; conflicting-source resolution; meeting-to-Action linkage; meeting-to-Decision linkage; meeting-to-Project-timeline linkage). **§6B four canonical access tiers** (NEVER collapsed): §6B.1 Internal Enterprise Access (SAME_ORG/HIVE/PROJECT/ACTION scope; TAR-authoritative; standard audit) + §6B.2 Compliance/Legal Review Access (`COMPLIANCE_REVIEW_SCOPED`; enhanced audit; privileged-conversation redaction-lift under attorney-client privilege review; jurisdiction-aware) + §6B.3 Regulator-Facing Evidence Package Access (ADR-0036 LawfulBasis 9-condition gate + ADR-0070 regulator-ready doctrine; export-only NEVER live drilldown; dual-control approval per ADR-0026; minimum-necessary discipline) + §6B.4 External Third-Party Access (counterparties/NDAs/discovery/contractual right; explicit per-party authorization NEVER inferred from same-org TAR; maximum audit; maximum redaction; NEVER signal-generation capability). **§6C capture-eligibility + work-relevance filtering layer** (sits architecturally BEFORE Layer 1 ingest; gates every downstream layer): §6C.1 8 pre-capture gates (approved meeting/channel/workspace + notice/consent + enterprise-owned-device + project/matter/client/action/hive scope + business purpose + retention policy + legal/compliance policy + privacy policy); §6C.2 5-class work-relevance classifier (biased toward privacy; `UNKNOWN_REQUIRES_REVIEW` default when uncertain); §6C.3 personal/protected-category exclusion list (family/medical/romantic/financial-hardship/religious-political/banter/lunch-social/personal-conflict/venting/emotional-state/psychological-inference/union-organizing/protected-class — NEVER signals); §6C.4 mixed-conversation handling (isolate work segment only; redact personal); §6C.5 sensitive-personal handling (BLOCKED from Agent Playground entirely unless legal hold requires retention under compliance scope only); §6C.6 11-value `business_purpose_label` vocab (PROJECT_CONTEXT/CLIENT_OR_CUSTOMER_WORK/ACTION_RELATED/APPROVAL_RELATED/COMPLIANCE_REVIEW/LEGAL_HOLD/INCIDENT_REVIEW/HIVE_OR_TEAM_COORDINATION/SALES_OR_ACCOUNT_WORK/SUPPORT_CASE/UNKNOWN_BUSINESS_PURPOSE); §6C.7 default Agent Playground consumption rule; §6C.8 default cockpit rule (no raw transcript by default); §6C.9 three filter-outcome vocabs (`conversation_relevance_class` 5 values + `capture_eligibility` 7 values + `agent_playground_use` 5 values); §6C.10 9-value `scope_binding_type` vocab; §6C.11 privacy-bias filtering standard; §6C.12 signal-shape additive fields (conversation_relevance_class + capture_eligibility + agent_playground_use + redaction_applied + business_purpose_label + scope_binding_type + review_required + personal_content_suppressed; REQUIRED on every signal); §6C.13 ADR-0079 prerequisite extension. **§7 five-stage implementation ladder** (Stage 0 this ADR LANDED 2026-05-31; Stage 1 Layer 1 schema + Layer 3 helper + Layer 4 read service requires ADR-0079; Stage 5 hierarchy + graph integration). **§8/§9 future Wave 7 + Wave 9 attachment points** (additive sidecar; bounded count recommended ≤8 per response). **§5 Wave 10 cockpit attachment** (replaces ADR-0077 §8.2 "not available" placeholder; Layer-4 drilldown ONLY = exact quotes + named attribution + raw timestamps when authorized; FORBIDDEN at every layer regardless of authorization = emotion/sentiment scoring + employee/manager/psychological scoring + legal/regulator certainty + manager-action prescriptions + cross-org fusion + raw audio/video/screen-capture + chain-of-thought + embeddings/vectors/content_hash/storage_location/bridge_id/secret_ref/connector_payload at response surface. **§12 audit posture**: ZERO new audit literal; suggested future `details.action` discriminators `CONVERSATION_CONTEXT_SIGNALS_READ` / `CONVERSATION_CONTEXT_SIGNAL_GENERATED` / `TRANSCRIPT_EXCERPT_DRILLDOWN_READ`; Layer-4 drilldown read events MUST emit audit row when `drilldown_audit_required` true (default true). **§13 regulator-ready posture**: ADR-0070 §9 legal-advice boundary inherited; signals MAY support evidence posture as closed-vocab metadata only ("policy concern raised" / "approval dependency identified" / etc.); signals MUST NEVER claim compliant/legally-sufficient/regulator-approved/no-fine-risk/employee-violated-policy/manager-failed-supervision; exact transcripts MAY be packaged as regulator evidence ONLY under ADR-0036 LawfulBasis 9-condition gate + §3.9 `REGULATOR_EVIDENCE_PACKAGE` + §6 Stage 3 prerequisites + minimum-necessary discipline. **§14 RULE 0 + same-org boundary universal**. **§15 ADR-0069 §6 8-question check** for Stage 3+ governed-listener implementation. **§16 wave-map alignment** preserves Section 2 / Wave 8 boundaries (Wave 8 NEVER bypassed; NO Action creation/execution at any layer; NO LLM-generated signal text without closed-vocab projection; NO numeric scoring/ranking/probability/employee scoring/manager surveillance/psychological profiling at any layer; NO default-render of raw transcript content at any Foundation API surface — only Layer 4 permissioned drilldown explicitly authorized renders authorized excerpts). **§17 forward queue** load-bearing: ADR-0079 Transcript Substrate Policy (MUST cover §6 + §6A + §6B + §6C). no cross-owner path); §9 bounded influence (Wave 6A v1 default 5 / cap 25 inherited; ~4-5 KB max response weight per call); §10 explicit owner-control opt-out (`include_alignment_patterns: false`); §11 audit posture — NO new audit literal (assembleContext emits zero writeAuditEvent calls; Wave 6B inherits this no-audit posture; Wave 5 ADR-0066 §7 audit covers the lifecycle write side); §12 v1 explicit non-goals (score-boost would require ADR-0022 amendment + Founder authorization; pre-filter keyword injection; capsule pipeline mutation; non-owner alignment_patterns exposure; LLM autonomy over pattern selection; auto-acceptance from inside assembleContext; per-conversation override beyond the boolean opt-out; bidirectional alignment proposal from inside conductSession; persistent usage analytics); §13 RULE 0 + symbiotic doctrine universal (user teaches Twin through review-and-acceptance; Twin reflects accepted patterns back as visible alignment memory; user remains sovereign; forbidden surfaces: employee scoring / surveillance / manager visibility / psychological profiling / compliance scoring / discipline / silent mutation / cross-owner / cross-org); §14 implementation slice estimate (4 code surfaces + ≥12 integration tests + zero schema migration + zero new audit literal). - **ADR-0066** — Section 1 Wave 5 — Otzar Proposed-Pattern from Recurring Drift (review-gated; design-only) (Section 1 Wave 5 contract ADR; **design-only — no code, no schema migration, no new routes, no new audit literal in this commit**. Closes ADR-0058 §"Forward queue" item 1 (`IntelligencePattern` auto-write from recurring correction themes) at the design register; implementation slice forward-substrate behind separate Founder authorization per Founder Wave 5 direction "If implementation requires new schema, stop after ADR and report exact model/fields needed." NEW Prisma model `OtzarProposedPattern` proposed (separate from existing org-scoped `IntelligencePattern` at `schema.prisma:1100-1114` which stays unchanged per RULE 1 — Phase 0 verified `IntelligencePattern` is actively used by `priming.ts:216` + `org.routes.ts:2369`, is org-scoped not owner-scoped, has free-form description + raw excerpt in evidence, and has wrong status lifecycle for Wave 5). 11 sub-decisions: §1 Wave 5 product purpose + scope lock (auto-write = auto-propose NOT auto-commit; NOT surveillance / NOT manager scoring / NOT psychological profiling / NOT hidden compliance scoring / NOT autonomous memory mutation / NOT cross-employee comparison / NOT cross-org aggregation / NOT LLM-generated proposal text / NOT raw correction or transcript exposure / NOT numeric drift score / NOT active pattern consumption); closed-vocab String columns (not Prisma enum) per Hive/MemoryCapsule/PlaygroundScenario precedent; NO description column + NO evidence Json + NO org_entity_id column (all deliberate); §4 closed-vocab discriminators + labels at v1 (`source_signal_type` ∈ PER_CONVERSATION_DRIFT|WALLET_STALE_CONTEXT|CROSS_CONVERSATION_ROLLUP; `pattern_label` ∈ RECURRING_CORRECTION_RECOMMENDATION_REVIEW|STALE_CONTEXT_REFRESH_RECOMMENDED|CROSS_CONVERSATION_ALIGNMENT_RECOMMENDED; `confidence_label` ∈ LOW|MEDIUM|HIGH; `status` ∈ PROPOSED|ACCEPTED|REJECTED|ARCHIVED); §5 recurrence-detection criteria (per-conversation drift ≥ 3 distinct convos in 14d window → MEDIUM, ≥ 6 → HIGH; wallet stale-context ≥ 7 consecutive days → MEDIUM, ≥ 14 → HIGH; cross-conversation rollup ≥ 7 consecutive days → MEDIUM, ≥ 14 → HIGH) + deduplication policy (no duplicate PROPOSED row while existing PROPOSED|ACCEPTED row is non-archived); §6 4-route review surface (`POST /api/v1/otzar/my-twin/proposed-patterns/sweep` + `GET /api/v1/otzar/my-twin/proposed-patterns` + `GET /api/v1/otzar/my-twin/proposed-patterns/:id` + `PATCH /api/v1/otzar/my-twin/proposed-patterns/:id`); bearer + "read" scope; cross-owner/unknown id → 404 PROPOSED_PATTERN_NOT_FOUND enumeration-safe; forbidden state transitions → 422 INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION; forbidden body fields on PATCH → 422 INVALID_REQUEST (only `status` updatable); §7 ADMIN_ACTION + details.action discriminator audit posture (5 discriminators: OTZAR_PATTERN_PROPOSED + OTZAR_PATTERN_READ + OTZAR_PATTERN_ACCEPTED + OTZAR_PATTERN_REJECTED + OTZAR_PATTERN_ARCHIVED); ZERO new audit literal; safe details only (action + pattern_id + owner_entity_id + source_signal_type + pattern_label + status + confidence_label); forbidden in audit row (safe_summary, raw correction text, raw transcript, raw capsule content, conversation IDs, topic tag values, embeddings, vectors, storage locations, content hashes, bridge IDs, secret refs, cross-owner/cross-org data, chain-of-thought, prompts, numeric scores); - **ADR-0064** — Section 3 Hives Wave 5 — Hive Events Producer Substrate (Section 3 Wave 5 contract ADR; **ADR-only at landing + producer-only implementation contingent if substrate-safe per §Sub-decision 13**. failed state transitions emit no events; (6) **Fire-and-forget delivery semantics** — no persistence + no retry queue + no outbox table + no external side effects at v1; handler failures swallowed silently to never block state transitions; (8) **Zero schema migration** — no new models, no event-persistence table, no outbox at v1; (9) **Single-node-safe topology at v1** — multi-node delivery NOT claimed; Phoenix.PubSub multi-node substrate (libcluster + PG2 at dbgi_supervisor) documented as substrate-present but not production-verified for Hive fanout; (10) **Cross-section integration boundaries** preserved — ADR-0002 audit chain stays source of truth; ADR-0028 future BEAM bridge inherits closed vocabulary + topic schema; ADR-0039 entry #28 producer half closed; Locks: (1) **v1 scope** — same-org-scoped, RULE 0-respecting intra-organization coordination; every Hive MUST have non-null `org_entity_id`; `hive_type` MUST be ENTERPRISE or PERSONAL_NETWORK; members MUST share Hive's org; aggregate is counts/labels only NEVER raw content NEVER per-member content attribution; (2) **NON-GOALS at v1** — Cross-organization Hives (collides with RULE 0; HiveType CROSS_ORGANIZATION + DEVICE_NETWORK + GOVERNMENT rejected at service tier), Twin-to-Twin proactive runtime (ADR-0052 §8; forward-substrate to Wave 8+), `governance_terms Json` policy enforcement (stored opaquely; forward-substrate), Hive admin routes (Wave 3+), Phoenix.PubSub fanout (ADR-0039 entry #28; Wave 5+), Broadway pipeline (Wave 6+), hive algorithm weighting (Wave 7+), AI-generated executive summaries (Founder product decision), cross-hive aggregation; `capsule_types_accessible` enforced at read-time (zero-state response for empty access); SAFE projection pattern mirrors ADR-0058 §7 drift signals; (4) **NO schema migration** — existing 12-field Hive + 10-field HiveMembership + 5 enums sufficient; (5) **NO new audit literal** — 5 HIVE_* literals (`HIVE_CREATED` + `HIVE_MEMBER_ADDED` + `HIVE_MEMBER_REMOVED` + `HIVE_INTELLIGENCE_READ` + `HIVE_AGGREGATE_BUILT`) already at audit.ts:50-54 suffice; (6) **5 Founder authorization checkpoints** required before Wave 2 implementation — scope-lock confirmation; auto-join semantics; TAR gate (BREAKING for un-gated callers); cross-org membership rejection (BREAKING for any cross-org caller); capsule-type filtering at read (BREAKING — surfaces zero-state where today operators get unfiltered aggregate); (7) **Patent-implementation evidence per RULE 19 + ADR-0020** — `aggregate_capsule_id` (US 12,517,919 capsule layer), `is_default_enterprise` (US 12,517,919 + US 12,164,537 + US 12,399,904 portability), `capsule_types_contributed/accessible` (US 12,517,919 capsule-layer permission). Substrate-honest correction: prior `docs/current-build-state/03-hives-team-intelligence.md` claimed "Substrate not yet started"; actual on-main state = Hive + HiveMembership models + HiveService (5 methods) + hive.routes.ts + 5 HIVE_* audit literals all LIVE. Cites ADR-0001 + ADR-0002 + ADR-0039 + ADR-0046 + ADR-0052 + ADR-0058 + RULE 0/4/13/14/19/20; Founder authorization explicit at `[FOUNDER-SLEEP-DIRECTIVE-SECTION-3-HIVES-V1-ADR-AUTH]` per Founder Sleep Directive 2026-05-30; Status: **Accepted 2026-05-30** by Founder Sleep Directive)

- **ADR-0058** — Otzar Drift Detection — Coaching/Alignment Trust Loop (Wave 3A contract ADR; **design-only — no code/endpoints/schema migration in this phase**; governed by ADR-0052 doctrine + closes ADR-0053 §5 Wave 3 forward queue + closes ADR-0055 Wave 3 drift detection ADR reservation. Locks: (1) **Coaching/alignment vs surveillance boundary** canonical — drift signals are self-scoped coaching prompts for the caller's own Twin; NEVER manager visibility, NEVER employee scoring, NEVER psychological inference, NEVER punitive policy enforcement, NEVER raw conversation content exposure; (2) **NO schema migration** — reuses ADR-0055 `MemoryCapsule.conversation_id` + existing `wallet_id` self-scope + existing `@@index([wallet_id, capsule_type, conversation_id])`; (3) **NO new audit literal** — emits `ADMIN_ACTION + details.action = DRIFT_SIGNAL_READ` per Section 7 + Section 4 Wave 2/4/5/7 precedent; (4) **Pure derived read-only service** — `DriftSignalService.analyzeConversationDrift` computes signals live from the caller's own CORRECTION capsules; NOT persisted as a separate "drift profile" row; (5) **Closed-vocabulary v1 signal labels** — `CORRECTION_VELOCITY_ELEVATED` (>3 CORRECTION capsules in conversation) + `RECURRING_CORRECTION_THEME` (2+ corrections share a non-generic topic tag); future labels add via additive extension behind separate slice authorization; (6) **NEW route** `GET /api/v1/otzar/conversations/:id/drift-signals` bearer + `read`; mirrors Wave 2C `/corrections` self-scope (cross-caller → 403 NOT_CONVERSATION_OWNER; unknown → 404 CONVERSATION_NOT_FOUND); (7) **SAFE projection** — `{ ok, conversation_id, drift_signals[{label, honest_note}], signal_count, corrections_observed, coaching_note, boundary_note }`; FORBIDDEN — raw correction text, capsule IDs, topic tag values, payload_summary, transcripts, numeric scores, per-employee comparison; (8) **Forward-substrate** (separate slice/authorization required) — stale-context drift (consumes ADR-0044/0045), role-scope conflict drift (consumes Section 2 ActionAttempt POLICY_DRIFT), org-wide aggregation, drift digest push via Section 4 connectors, operator-tunable thresholds, cross-conversation Twin-level rollup, IntelligencePattern auto-write, Control Tower drift UX; cites RULE 0 + RULE 4 + RULE 9 + RULE 13 + RULE 20 + ADR-0044 + ADR-0045 + ADR-0052 + ADR-0053 + ADR-0055 + ADR-0057 §10; Founder authorization explicit at `[FOUNDER-SLEEP-DIRECTIVE-SECTION-1-WAVE-3-OTZAR-DRIFT-DETECTION-AUTH]` per Founder Sleep Directive 2026-05-30; Status: **Accepted 2026-05-30** by Founder Sleep Directive)

ADRs are sequentially numbered. Gaps are not closed when ADRs
are superseded or deprecated — a retired ADR keeps its number
with Status updated to "Superseded by ADR-NNNN" or "Deprecated."
This preserves citation stability across the ADR catalog over
time.

## ADR Lifecycle

Status flows: **Proposed** → **Accepted YYYY-MM-DD** → optionally
**Superseded by ADR-NNNN** or **Deprecated**.

Add a new ADR when an architectural decision is one that future
contributors will need to understand the rationale for. If a
decision is purely tactical and won't be referenced in six
months, it doesn't need an ADR.

Amend an existing ADR (in-place edit, same commit, no Status
change) for clarifications or to add new bidirectional
citations. Supersede an existing ADR (new ADR with explicit
"Supersedes ADR-NNNN" line, prior ADR's Status updated) when
a new architectural decision replaces an earlier one.

## Bidirectional Citation Discipline

Every ADR's References section ends with a "Bidirectional
citations (cited from)" block listing every other file that
cites it — glossary entries, architectural-anchors catalog
entries, other ADRs, code JSDoc comments. When adding a new
ADR that cites an existing ADR, the existing ADR's References
must be amended in the same commit to include the
back-citation.

The discipline ensures future readers grepping any file in the
citation graph can navigate to every related file. Broken
cross-references surface as missing back-citations during
review.

The two primary citation sources outside of ADRs themselves are
`docs/reference/glossary.md` (terminology + capitalization
conventions) and `docs/reference/architectural-anchors.md` (the
runtime-enforced architectural properties locked by tests).
